    > Multi-Select
        Supported features:
        Keyboard navigation (arrows, page up/down, home/end, space).
        Ctrl modifier to preserve and toggle selection.
        Shift modifier for range selection.
        Ctrl+A to select all.
        Escape to clear selection.
        Click and drag to box-select.
        Tip: Use 'Demo->Tools->Debug Log->Selection' to see selection requests as they happen.
        Selection: 4/50

        style.FontScaleMain = 1.00
        style.FontScaleDpi = 1.00
        global_scale = ~1.00
        FontSize = 18.00---
        { 22 } custom_size
        ImGui::PushFont(nullptr, custom_size);
        FontSize = 22.00 (== 22.00 * global_scale)---
        { 1.95 } custom_scale
        ImGui::PushFont(nullptr, style.FontSizeBase * custom_scale);
        FontSize = 35.00 (== style.FontSizeBase * 1.95 * global_scale)---
        FontSize = 9.00 (== style.FontSizeBase * 0.50 * global_scale)
        FontSize = 18.00 (== style.FontSizeBase * 1.00 * global_scale)
        FontSize = 27.00 (== style.FontSizeBase * 1.50 * global_scale)
        FontSize = 36.00 (== style.FontSizeBase * 2.00 * global_scale)
        FontSize = 45.00 (== style.FontSizeBase * 2.50 * global_scale)
        FontSize = 54.00 (== style.FontSizeBase * 3.00 * global_scale)

    Filter usage:
      ""         display all lines
      "xxx"      display lines containing "xxx"
      "xxx,yyy"  display lines containing "xxx" or "yyy"
      "-xxx"     hide lines containing "xxx"

        (?)

        [ ] ImGuiInputTextFlags_WordWrap (?)
        [x] ImGuiInputTextFlags_AllowTabInput (?)
        [ ] ImGuiInputTextFlags_CtrlEnterForNewLine
        { /*
         The Pentium F00F bug, shorthand for F0 0F C7 C8,
         the hexadecimal encoding of one offending instruction,
         more formally, the invalid operand with locked CMPXCHG8B
         instruction bug, is a design flaw in the majority of
         Intel Pentium, Pentium MMX, and Pentium OverDrive
         processors (all in the P5 microarchitecture).
        */
        
        label:
        	lock cmpxchg8b eax
        }
